in the following code, barL0 is (in Java2D coordinates) the LEFT end of the bar for a horizontal bar chart, and the TOP end of the bar for a vertical bar chart. Whether this is the BASE of the bar or not depends also on (a) whether the data value is 'negative' relative to the base value and (b) whether or not the range axis is inverted.
